Profile 
Sevenseas established in the year 2001 is over a decade old company operating out of India with a Pan India presence of 16 own offices covering all the major gateways in India. With an employee strength of over 350 and service portfolio which covers Import / Export freight forwarding by Air / Ocean , Customs Brokerage , Warehousing, Project cargo movement and Domestic Transportation, Sevenseas easily can claim to be the ideal partner in India for all logistics needs end to end. Sevenseas operates with all the necessary trade affiliations like IATA, FIATA, MTO & CUSTOMS BROKERAGE LICENCE . With a fleet of modern vehicles operating across India and extending into the west the growth pattern is very progressive. A very detailed outlay of Sevenseas is available at www.sevenseasexpress.com where one can find all the details as also downloadable presentations and monthly Newsletter copy.
Sevenseas has been awarded the ISO quality certification , effective Feb 2014 we are an ISO 9001 2008 Company

Profile 
Sevenseas established in the year 2001 is over a decade old company operating out of India with a Pan India presence of 16 own offices covering all the major gateways in India. With an employee strength of over 350 and service portfolio which covers Import / Export freight forwarding by Air / Ocean , Customs Brokerage , Warehousing, Project cargo movement and Domestic Transportation, Sevenseas easily can claim to be the ideal partner in India for all logistics needs end to end. Sevenseas operates with all the necessary trade affiliations like IATA, FIATA, MTO & CUSTOMS BROKERAGE LICENCE . With a fleet of modern vehicles operating across India and extending into the west the growth pattern is very progressive. A very detailed outlay of Sevenseas is available at www.sevenseasexpress.com where one can find all the details as also downloadable presentations and monthly Newsletter copy.
Sevenseas has been awarded the ISO quality certification , effective Feb 2014 we are an ISO 9001 2008 Company

On Time Express Ltd. was founded in 1995 and has grown from a local forwarder to a regional freight forwarding and logistics provider with over nine hundred employees, offices in 15 countries and about 43 locations in Asia and Dubai. Our headquarters are in Hong Kong, and our other offices include China, Thailand, Korea, Taiwan, Vietnam, Malaysia, Indonesia, Singapore, Sri Lanka, India , Cambodia , Bangladesh , Japan and Dubai . Within our extensive network in China, we have 15 offices; this gives us the ability to handle any inquiries you may have.
On Time offers a full range of services including air and sea freight forwarding, sea-air services, hand carry, high fashion hanging garment transportation, warehousing, insurance, customs clearance, free-domicile deliveries and logistical distribution services. With a state of the art Freight Management system, we are confident that On Time has the ability to provide a one stop shop for all of your forwarding and logistics needs.
